    15	class CiphertextHandle {
    16	public:
    17	    CiphertextHandle() = default;
    18	    explicit CiphertextHandle(Ciphertext<DCRTPoly> ct) : ct_(std::move(ct)) {}
    19	
    20	    bool valid() const {
    21	        return static_cast<bool>(ct_);
    22	    }
    23	
    24	    std::size_t level() const {
    25	        require_valid();
    26	        return ct_->GetLevel();
    27	    }
    28

    30	        require_valid();

    35	    friend class FidesCKKSContext;
    36

    40	        }
    41	    }
    42	
    43	    Ciphertext<DCRTPoly> ct_;

    46	class FidesCKKSContext {

    86	        }
    87	
    88	        cc_ = GenCryptoContext(params);
    89	        cc_->Enable(PKE);
    90	        cc_->Enable(KEYSWITCH);
    91	        cc_->Enable(LEVELEDSHE);
    92	
    93	        auto kp = cc_->KeyGen();
    94	        if (!kp.publicKey || !kp.secretKey) {
    95	            throw std::runtime_error("KeyGen failed");
    96	        }
    97	
    98	        pk_ = kp.publicKey;
    99	        sk_ = kp.secretKey;
   100	
   101	        if (with_mult_key) {
   102	            cc_->EvalMultKeyGen(sk_);
   103	        }
   104	
   105	        if (!rotation_steps.empty()) {
   106	            cc_->EvalRotateKeyGen(sk_, rotation_steps);
   107	        }
   108	
   109	        cc_->LoadContext(pk_);
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    py::dict info() const {
   113	        require_ready();
   114	        py::dict d;
   115	        d["ring_dim"] = cc_->GetRingDimension();
   116	        d["cyclotomic_order"] = cc_->GetCyclotomicOrder();
   117	        return d;
   118	    }
   119	
   120	    CiphertextHandle encrypt(const std::vector<double>& x) {
   121	        require_ready();
   122	        auto pt = cc_->MakeCKKSPackedPlaintext(x);
   123	        auto ct = cc_->Encrypt(pt, pk_);
   124	        pt.reset();
   125	        return CiphertextHandle(ct);
   126	    }
   127	
   128	    std::vector<double> decrypt(CiphertextHandle& h, std::size_t logical_length = 0) {
   129	        require_ready();
   130	        h.require_valid();
   131	
   132	        Plaintext pt_dec;
   133	        auto dec_res = cc_->Decrypt(h.ct_, sk_, &pt_dec);
   134	        if (!dec_res.isValid) {
   135	            throw std::runtime_error("Decrypt failed");
   136	        }
   137	
   138	        if (logical_length > 0) {
   139	            pt_dec->SetLength(logical_length);
   140	        }
   141	
   142	        auto out = pt_dec->GetRealPackedValue();
   143	        pt_dec.reset();
   144	        return out;
   145	    }
   146	
   147	    CiphertextHandle eval_add_ct(const CiphertextHandle& a, const CiphertextHandle& b) {
   148	        require_ready();
   149	        a.require_valid();
   150	        b.require_valid();
   151	
   152	        auto ct_out = cc_->EvalAdd(a.ct_, b.ct_);
   153	        return CiphertextHandle(ct_out);
   154	    }
   155	
   156	    CiphertextHandle eval_add_plain_ct(const CiphertextHandle& a, const std::vector<double>& plain) {
   157	        require_ready();
   158	        a.require_valid();
   159	
   160	        auto pt = cc_->MakeCKKSPackedPlaintext(plain);
   161	        auto ct_out = cc_->EvalAdd(a.ct_, pt);
   162	        pt.reset();
   163	        return CiphertextHandle(ct_out);
   164	    }
   165	
   166	    CiphertextHandle eval_mult_scalar_ct(const CiphertextHandle& a, double scalar) {
   167	        require_ready();
   168	        a.require_valid();
   169	
   170	        auto ct_out = cc_->EvalMult(a.ct_, scalar);
   171	        return CiphertextHandle(ct_out);
   172	    }
   173	
   174	    CiphertextHandle eval_mult_plain_ct(const CiphertextHandle& a, const std::vector<double>& plain) {
   175	        require_ready();
   176	        a.require_valid();
   177	
   178	        auto pt = cc_->MakeCKKSPackedPlaintext(plain);
   179	        auto ct_out = cc_->EvalMult(a.ct_, pt);
   180	        pt.reset();
   181	        return CiphertextHandle(ct_out);
   182	    }
   183	
   184	    CiphertextHandle eval_rotate_ct(const CiphertextHandle& a, int steps) {
   185	        require_ready();
   186	        a.require_valid();
   187	
   188	        auto ct_out = cc_->EvalRotate(a.ct_, steps);
   189	        return CiphertextHandle(ct_out);
   190	    }
   191	
   192	    std::vector<double> roundtrip(const std::vector<double>& x) {
   193	        auto ct = encrypt(x);
   194	        return decrypt(ct, x.size());
   195	    }
   196	
   197	    std::vector<double> eval_add(const std::vector<double>& x, const std::vector<double>& y) {
   198	        require_ready();
   199	
   200	        if (x.size() != y.size()) {
   201	            throw std::runtime_error("eval_add(): x and y must have the same length");
   202	        }
   203	
   204	        auto ct_x = encrypt(x);
   205	        auto ct_y = encrypt(y);
   206	        auto ct_sum = eval_add_ct(ct_x, ct_y);
   207	        return decrypt(ct_sum, x.size());
   208	    }
   209	
   210	    std::vector<double> eval_mult_scalar(const std::vector<double>& x, double scalar) {
   211	        require_ready();
   212	
   213	        auto ct_x = encrypt(x);
   214	        auto ct_mul = eval_mult_scalar_ct(ct_x, scalar);
   215	        return decrypt(ct_mul, x.size());
   216	    }
   217	
   218	    void close() {
   219	        if (sk_) sk_.reset();
   220	        if (pk_) pk_.reset();
   221	        if (cc_) cc_.reset();
   222	        (void)cudaDeviceSynchronize();
   223	    }
   224	
   225	private:
   226	    void require_ready() const {
   227	        if (!cc_ || !pk_ || !sk_) {
   228	            throw std::runtime_error("FidesCKKSContext is not initialized");
   229	        }
   230	    }
   231	
   232	    CryptoContext<DCRTPoly> cc_;
   233	    PublicKey<DCRTPoly> pk_;
   234	    PrivateKey<DCRTPoly> sk_;
   235	};
   236	
   237	PYBIND11_MODULE(_fideslib, m) {
   238	    m.doc() = "pybind11 bindings for FIDESlib";
   239	
   240	    py::class_<CiphertextHandle>(m, "CiphertextHandle")
   241	        .def(py::init<>())
   242	        .def("valid", &CiphertextHandle::valid)
   243	        .def("level", &CiphertextHandle::level)
   244	        .def("noise_scale_deg", &CiphertextHandle::noise_scale_deg);
   245	
   246	    py::class_<FidesCKKSContext>(m, "FidesCKKSContext")
   247	        .def(py::init<>())
   248	
   249	        .def(
   250	            "init",
   251	            &FidesCKKSContext::init,
   252	            py::arg("multiplicative_depth") = 2,
   253	            py::arg("scaling_mod_size") = 50,
   254	            py::arg("batch_size") = 8,
   255	            py::arg("ring_dim") = (1u << 14),
   256	            py::arg("first_mod_size") = -1,
   257	            py::arg("num_large_digits") = -1,
   258	            py::arg("devices") = std::vector<int>{0},
   259	            py::arg("plaintext_autoload") = true,
   260	            py::arg("ciphertext_autoload") = true,
